I need to analyze each candidate to determine if it can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `0.1728*(1 - P/48.55)*P + 0.1728*P/(1 + exp(-1.524*(-0.924 + P)))`

Simplifying GT:
- First term: `0.1728*P - 0.003559*P²` (a linear + quadratic in P)
- Second term: `0.1728*P/(1 + exp(-1.524*P + 1.408))` (a sigmoidal term in P)

Key features of GT:
1. **P² term** (negative coefficient)
2. **P term** (positive coefficient)
3. **Sigmoid-like term**: `P/(1 + exp(f(P)))` — this is a function of P only
4. **No dependence on t** — GT is independent of t
5. No constant term (when P=0, GT=0)

For candidates with `t` dependence, I need to check if all `t`-dependent terms can be zeroed out.

The sigmoid term `P/(1 + exp(-c5*(P - c6)))` is a key structural element. Let me check which candidates can reproduce this.

**Critical analysis of the sigmoid term:**
The term `0.1728*P/(1 + exp(-1.524*(P - 0.924)))` cannot be expressed as a polynomial, exponential, logarithmic, power law, or simple rational function of P. It requires a logistic/sigmoid structure.

Let me go through each candidate systematically:

**Candidate 1:** `P²*c0 + P²*c1 + P*c2 + P^c3*c4 + P^c5*c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)`
- Set c7=0 to eliminate t. Becomes `P²*(c0+c1) + P*c2 + c4*P^c3 + c6*P^c5`
- This is a sum of power functions of P. Cannot match sigmoid. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 2:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3) + c4*t/(c5+t) + c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)`
- Set c4=0, c7=0 to eliminate t. `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3) + c6`
- Has `P*exp(P*c3)` but GT has `P/(1+exp(f(P)))`. These are structurally different. Cannot match. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 3:** `P²*(c0+c1+c2+c3) + P*(c4+c5+c6+c7) + c8*t*exp(c9*t)`
- Set c8=0. Pure polynomial in P (quadratic). Cannot match sigmoid. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 4:** `P*c0*Max(0, P+c1) + P*c2 + c3*t*exp(c4*t)`
- Set c3=0. `P*c0*Max(0, P+c1) + P*c2`
- Max function is piecewise linear, not sigmoid. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 5:** `P²*c0 + P²*c1 + P*c2 + P^c3*c4 + P^c5*c6 + c7*t*exp(c8*t)`
- Same as Candidate 1 with different t term. Set c7=0. Power functions, no sigmoid. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 6:** `P*c0*Max(0,P+c1) + P*c2 + P*c3 + P^c4*c5 + c6*exp(c7*t) + c8*log(c9*t+1)/P^5`
- Set c6=0, c8=0. Piecewise + power functions. No sigmoid. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 7:** Similar to 6 with extra t terms. Set t-terms to 0. No sigmoid. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 8:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*Max(0, P*c3-1) + P^c4*c5*exp(P*c6) + c7*t*exp(c8*t)`
- Set c7=0. Has `P^c4*c5*exp(P*c6)` — not sigmoid form. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 9-50:** Let me check for any candidate that has a sigmoid-like structure `P/(1+exp(f(P)))` or equivalent.

Looking through all candidates, I see terms like:
- `P*c/(P*c+1)` (rational, not sigmoid)
- `P*exp(P*c)` (not sigmoid)
- `Max(0,...)` (piecewise linear)
- `log(P*c+1)` (logarithmic)
- `P/(P+c)` (rational)

None of these can replicate `P/(1+exp(f(P)))` which is a true sigmoid function. The sigmoid is linearly independent from all polynomial, rational, exponential, logarithmic, and power-law basis functions.

After careful review of all 50 candidates, **none** contain a sigmoid/logistic function structure that could match `P/(1+exp(-c*(P-c)))`.
